if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') != '7244e5cb7c680f5c60e773877a057211069edd90') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '7244e5cb7c680f5c60e773877a057211069edd90') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== 'e4117c4feb665613995f4fe78bef861ca30433da') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '7244e5cb7c680f5c60e773877a057211069edd90') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql') != '87911f57edd494641a2102496da34ecc231c8426') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql') !== '87911f57edd494641a2102496da34ecc231c8426') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql') !== 'f0f77ee1242b9b59120034d1cf5d859733da61a5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql') !== '87911f57edd494641a2102496da34ecc231c8426') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_other.sql');
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt') != '6f42dc66d765fe6aed028f58bdc2fb93ff1fb4d0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt') !== '6f42dc66d765fe6aed028f58bdc2fb93ff1fb4d0') {
		if (@sha1_file('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt') !== '6945d96ad09cd4eec55b6e107492b5bb7d9d47c4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt') !== '6f42dc66d765fe6aed028f58bdc2fb93ff1fb4d0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois-00.txt');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('whois/webwhois.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: whois/webwhois.php');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('whois/webwhois.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): whois/webwhois.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('whois/webwhois.php') != '6857b9ec5a334b261ed023b56f425b6f562b7c0a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): whois/webwhois.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('whois/webwhois.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of whois/webwhois.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('whois/webwhois.php') !== '6857b9ec5a334b261ed023b56f425b6f562b7c0a') {
		if (@sha1_file('whois/webwhois.php') !== '13035da0550df43dbb04e80a1b52e784490ad4fd') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: whois/webwhois.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('whois/webwhois.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('whois/webwhois.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('whois/webwhois.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('whois/webwhois.php') !== '6857b9ec5a334b261ed023b56f425b6f562b7c0a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): whois/webwhois.php');
		}
	}
}
